      *--------------------------------------------------------------*
      * Funzione :  Calcolo domande  DS ordinaria                    *
      *                                                              *
      * PGM Chiamante : -------->  PDSIO01                           *
      * PGM chiamati:                                                *
      *             PDSIO02    per calcolo DS                        *
      *             PDSPD16    per gestione lavori struttura         *
      *             RDSUT11    per msg a video                       *
      *             RDSUT13    per decodifica comuni                 *
      *             RDSUT15    per Anagrafica                        *
      *             RDSJOB1    per modifica cola lavori              *
      *             RDSUSR1    per identif. utente                   *
      *             RDSERR0    per mappa errori                      *
      *             RDSOR12    per strutture attive                  *
      *      ex     PNPGFE0    per gestione fiscale                  *
      *      new    PNPGFD0    per gestione fiscale                  *
      *             RNPYEAR    per data                              *
      *                                                              *
      * Dati ricevuti :  L-AREA                                      *
      * Dati passati  :  L-AREA                                      *
      *                                                              *
      * ARCHIVI        :  Input/Output                               *
      *  1  video      -   MDSPD13    -  Mappa video                 *
      *  2  RIEPILOGO  -   ADSRPG00   -  Riepilogo pagamenti G00     *
      *  3  DATICOMUNI -   LFDATCO2   -  logico su ADSDATCO          *
      *  4  RECUPERI       ADSRECUP   -  File recuperi               *
      *  5  EFFEROGATI     LFPEERE1   -  Logico su ADSPEERE          *
      *  6  APPOGGIO       ADSAPIO0   -  Analitico Pagamenti         *
      *  7  FILE40         ADSASU     -  file Enti                   *
      *  8  FILE42         ADSASU2    -  file Delibere               *
      *  9  FILE47         ADSASU7    -  file anagrafiche lavoratori *
      * 10  FILE48         ADSASU8    -  file liste lavoratori       *
      * 11  FILE49         ADSASU9    -  file dati contabili pagament*
      * 12  FILE51         ADSATTSU   -  file Assegno ASU            *
      * 13  FILE52         ADSLAVPU   -  file Lav.Pubblica Utilità   *
      * 14  FILE53         ADSSUSST   -  file Sussidio Straordinario *
      * 22  SITUAZIODO     ADSSITDO   -  Situazione domanda          *
      *                                                              *
      * ARCHIVI        :  Input                                      *
      * 15  LRIEPILOGO -   LDSRPG01   -  logico su ADSRPG00          *
      * 16  ANAGRAFICI     ADSDATAN   -  File dati anagrafici        *
      * 17  DELEGHE        LFDELSI1   -  Logico su ADSDELSI          *
      * 18  DATIANF        LFMODAN1   -  Logico si ADSMODAN          *
      * 19  FILE64         ADSPERIO   -  Periodi LSU/LPU/BL          *
      * ??  L02COMUNI  -   LFDATCO2   -  logico su dati-comuni       *
      * 20  FILE65         ADSSX00    -  Tabella categorie           *
      * 23  FILE66         LFSOSPE1   -  Vista tabella sospensioni   *
      *                                                              *
      * ARCHIVI        :  Output                                     *
      * 21  STAMPA         SDSPD13    -  File di stampa              *
      *
      * ARCHIVI        :  non usare                                  *
      * xx  PAGAMENTI      ADSPAGME   -  non usato                   *
      * xx  DSCOMUNI       ADSDACOD   -  non usato                   *
      * xx  TEOEROGABI     LFPEERT1   -  non usato                   *
      * xx  PENSIONI       ADSPENSI   -  non usato                   *

      ******************************************************************
      *       DECLARE DEI CURSORI
      ******************************************************************
      *
      * FLAG SELEZIONE CURSORE
      * 1  = 1 RANGE
      * 2=2 RANGE
      * ...
      *
       01  WK-CURS          PIC X VALUE '1'.
      *
       01  C-IND            PIC 9.
      *
           EXEC SQL
              DECLARE  CURSDCO1 CURSOR   WITH HOLD FOR
              SELECT
                    H_DCOCODFIS,
                    H_DCOCENOPE,
                    H_DCOCOTIDO,
                    H_DCOCHIDOM,
                    H_DCOPENS,
                    H_DCOANFRIC,
                    H_DCOANVEPR,
                    H_DCONDVEPR,
                    H_DCOULESPP,
                    H_DCODTULPP,
                    H_DCOULESSP,
                    H_DCODTULSP,
                    H_DCODTPRDO,
                    H_DCODTDECPP,
                    H_DCODTDECSP,
                    H_DCOCODPAT,
                    H_DCOZONPAT,
                    H_DCOMODARR,
                    H_DCOCOOBAN,
                    H_DCOCOREIM,
                    H_DCOTRDOCE,
                    H_DCODTCODO,
                    H_DCODTVIR,
                    H_DCOINT,
                    H_DCORECNUO,
                    H_DCODTADEC,
                    H_DCOPESTDI,
                    H_DCOTRDODO,
                    H_DCOCOERMI,
                    H_DCODORICO,
                    H_DCOFLASU,
                    H_DCONUPRO,
                    H_DCOIBAN

               FROM    TDSDATCO
               WHERE
                H_DCOCOTIDO IN ('B', 'D', 'E')  AND
                H_DCOULESSP IN ('L', 'A')       AND
                H_DCOCOREIM = 0                 AND
                H_DCOPESTDI =      'S'          AND
                H_DCOCENOPE =      :H-DCOCENOPE AND
                H_DCOCOSEGR =      :H-DCOCOSEGR AND
                H_DCONDVEPR BETWEEN
                 :NUMERO-DAL-IN1 AND :NUMERO-AL-IN1  AND
                H_DCOANVEPR BETWEEN
                 :ANNO-DAL-IN1  AND   :ANNO-AL-IN1
               ORDER BY H_DCOANVEPR, H_DCONDVEPR
           END-EXEC.
      *
           EXEC SQL
              DECLARE  CURSDCO2 CURSOR   WITH HOLD FOR
              SELECT
                    H_DCOCODFIS,
                    H_DCOCENOPE,
                    H_DCOCOTIDO,
                    H_DCOCHIDOM,
                    H_DCOPENS,
                    H_DCOANFRIC,
                    H_DCOANVEPR,
                    H_DCONDVEPR,
                    H_DCOULESPP,
                    H_DCODTULPP,
                    H_DCOULESSP,
                    H_DCODTULSP,
                    H_DCODTPRDO,
                    H_DCODTDECPP,
                    H_DCODTDECSP,
                    H_DCOCODPAT,
                    H_DCOZONPAT,
                    H_DCOMODARR,
                    H_DCOCOOBAN,
                    H_DCOCOREIM,
                    H_DCOTRDOCE,
                    H_DCODTCODO,
                    H_DCODTVIR,
                    H_DCOINT,
                    H_DCORECNUO,
                    H_DCODTADEC,
                    H_DCOPESTDI,
                    H_DCOTRDODO,
                    H_DCOCOERMI,
                    H_DCODORICO,
                    H_DCOFLASU,
                    H_DCONUPRO,
                    H_DCOIBAN

               FROM    TDSDATCO
               WHERE
                H_DCOCOTIDO IN ('B', 'D', 'E')  AND
                H_DCOULESSP IN ('L', 'A')       AND
                H_DCOCOREIM = 0                 AND
                H_DCOPESTDI =      'S'          AND
                H_DCOCENOPE =      :H-DCOCENOPE AND
                H_DCOCOSEGR =      :H-DCOCOSEGR AND
                (( H_DCONDVEPR BETWEEN
                 :NUMERO-DAL-IN1 AND :NUMERO-AL-IN1  AND
                   H_DCOANVEPR BETWEEN
                 :ANNO-DAL-IN1  AND   :ANNO-AL-IN1)  OR
                 ( H_DCONDVEPR BETWEEN
                 :NUMERO-DAL-IN2 AND :NUMERO-AL-IN2  AND
                   H_DCOANVEPR BETWEEN
                 :ANNO-DAL-IN2  AND   :ANNO-AL-IN2))
               ORDER BY H_DCOANVEPR, H_DCONDVEPR
           END-EXEC.

                    H_DCOCODFIS,

                    H_DCONDVEPR,
                    H_DCOULESPP,
                    H_DCODTULPP,

                    H_DCODTDECSP,

                    H_DCODTADEC,

                    H_DCOCOERMI,
                    H_DCODORICO,
                    H_DCOFLASU,
                    H_DCONUPRO,
                    H_DCOIBAN

               FROM    TDSDATCO
               WHERE
                H_DCOCOTIDO IN ('B', 'D', 'E')  AND
                H_DCOULESSP IN ('L', 'A')       AND
                H_DCOCOREIM = 0                 AND
                H_DCOPESTDI =      'S'          AND
                H_DCOCENOPE =      :H-DCOCENOPE AND
                H_DCOCOSEGR =      :H-DCOCOSEGR AND
                (( H_DCONDVEPR BETWEEN
                 :NUMERO-DAL-IN1 AND :NUMERO-AL-IN1  AND
                   H_DCOANVEPR BETWEEN
                 :ANNO-DAL-IN1  AND   :ANNO-AL-IN1)  OR
                 ( H_DCONDVEPR BETWEEN
                 :NUMERO-DAL-IN2 AND :NUMERO-AL-IN2  AND

               ORDER BY H_DCOANVEPR, H_DCONDVEPR
           END-EXEC.

               WHERE
                H_DCOCOTIDO IN ('B', 'D', 'E')  AND
                H_DCOULESSP IN ('L', 'A')       AND
                H_DCOCOREIM = 0                 AND
                H_DCOPESTDI =      'S'          AND
                H_DCOCENOPE =      :H-DCOCENOPE AND
                H_DCOCOSEGR =      :H-DCOCOSEGR AND
                (( H_DCONDVEPR BETWEEN
                 :NUMERO-DAL-IN1 AND :NUMERO-AL-IN1  AND
                   H_DCOANVEPR BETWEEN
                 :ANNO-DAL-IN1  AND   :ANNO-AL-IN1)  OR
                 ( H_DCONDVEPR BETWEEN
                 :NUMERO-DAL-IN2 AND :NUMERO-AL-IN2  AND
                   H_DCOANVEPR BETWEEN
                 :ANNO-DAL-IN2  AND   :ANNO-AL-IN2)  OR
                 ( H_DCONDVEPR BETWEEN
                 :NUMERO-DAL-IN3 AND :NUMERO-AL-IN3  AND
                   H_DCOANVEPR BETWEEN
                 :ANNO-DAL-IN3  AND   :ANNO-AL-IN3)  OR
                 ( H_DCONDVEPR BETWEEN
                 :NUMERO-DAL-IN4 AND :NUMERO-AL-IN4  AND
                    H_DCOANVEPR BETWEEN
                  :ANNO-DAL-IN4  AND   :ANNO-AL-IN4)  OR
                  ( H_DCONDVEPR BETWEEN
                  :NUMERO-DAL-IN5 AND :NUMERO-AL-IN5  AND
                    H_DCOANVEPR BETWEEN
                  :ANNO-DAL-IN5  AND   :ANNO-AL-IN5))
               ORDER BY H_DCOANVEPR, H_DCONDVEPR
           END-EXEC.

      *LINKAGE SECTION.

      *01  DFHCOMMAREA                PIC X(27000).
      *==============================================================*
       PROCEDURE  DIVISION
                            USING  COMMAREADS.
       MAIN.
      *
      *    DISPLAY '**** PDSIO13 **** '.
      *
           move spaces   to COMMAREADS-OUT.
      *
           MOVE   K-AREA       TO L-AREA.
           MOVE   KARAMETRI-IN TO PARAMETRI-IN.
           MOVE   KAREA-D      TO LAREA-D.
      *    display 'L-AREA       ' L-AREA.
      *    display 'PARAMETRI-IN ' PARAMETRI-IN.
      *    display ' LAREA-D     ' LAREA-D.
      *
           MOVE   K-PROCEDURA  TO OUT-PROCEDURA.
      *
           perform  I00-INIZIALI      thru  I00-EX.
      *                                                              *
           perform  C00-CENTRALI      thru  C00-EX.
      *                                                              *
           perform  F00-FINALI        thru  F00-EX.
      *                                                              *
           MOVE   COMMAREADS-OUT      TO COMMAREADS.
      *                                                              *
       MAIN-EX.
           GOBACK.
      *                                                              *
       B20-PERSTART.
           MOVE  'B20-PERSTART' TO  WABNDB-LABEL.
           move  'N'                  to  W-ERRORE.
           move  zeros                to  FST-LFDATCO2.
      *--------------------------------- Chiave record iniziale      *
      *    move  'L'             to  H-DCOULESSP
           move  L-CODICE-STOP   to  H-DCOCENOPE
           move  zeros           to  H-DCOANVEPR
                                     H-DCONDVEPR
                                     WIC-DOMANDA.
           move  W-DOMANDA-DAL   to  WIC-DOMANDA.
           subtract  1          from WIC-DOMANDA.
           move  WIC-ANNO        to  H-DCOANVEPR .
           move  WIC-NUMERO      to  H-DCONDVEPR .
      *
      * modifica per trattare tutte le domanda con anno<>aano1
      *
           if  TIPO-ELABO-IN   =  1
           then
               move  1           to NUMERO-DAL-IN1
           end-if.
      *--------------------------------  File dati comuni (LFDATCO2) *
           PERFORM B20-DB2-DECL-CURS     THRU  B20-DB2-DECL-CURS-EX.
      *
           PERFORM  B20-DB2-FETCH    THRU  B20-DB2-FETCH-EX.
           IF  SQLCODE =    0
               move  'S'              to   WL-DATICOMUNI
               move  H-DCOANVEPR  to   WIC-ANNO
               move  H-DCONDVEPR  to   WIC-NUMERO
               add  1  to   CTR-LET-DATCO
           ELSE
               PERFORM DATICOMUNI-DB2-CLSCUR THRU
                       DATICOMUNI-DB2-CLSCUR-EX
               move  'N'              to   WL-DATICOMUNI
               move  '96'             to  OUT-STATUS
               perform  T18-TESTO18   thru  T18-EX
               perform  W10-MSGERRORE thru  W10-EX
           END-IF.
       B20-EX.
           exit.
      *
       C00-CENTRALI.
           if  W-ERRORE  =  'N'
           then
               continue
           else
               go  to  C00-EX
           end-if.
      *
           if  TIPO-ELABO-IN  <  3
           then
               perform  B20-PERSTART     thru  B20-EX
               if  FST-LFDATCO2  =  0
               then
                   move  'N'    to  W-FINE-INTERVALLO
                   perform  E00-ELABORA       thru  E00-EX
                     until  W-FINE-INTERVALLO  =  'S'
               end-if
           end-if.
      *
           move  'S'   to  W-FINE-ELABORA.
           perform  E60-SINCRONIZZO  thru  E60-EX.
      *
       C00-EX.
           exit.
      *
       E00-ELABORA.
      *
           if  WL-DATICOMUNI  =  'S'
           then
               perform  E20-ELABORA20  thru  E20-EX
           end-if.
      *
           if  W-NIK  =  'S'
           then
               if  W-CHK-CAMPI  = spaces
               then
                   continue
               else
                   perform  S20-ELENCA       thru  S20-EX
               end-if
            end-if.
      *-------------------------------------Sincronizzo ogni record
           if  WL-DATICOMUNI  =  'S'
           then
      *        if  WS-APPOGGIO  =  'S'
      *        then
                   perform  E60-SINCRONIZZO  thru  E60-EX
      *        end-if
               if  W-FINE-INTERVALLO  =  'S'
               then
                   go  to  E00-EX
               end-if
           end-if.
           perform  E15-INIZIALIZZO  thru  E15-EX .
300320*------------------- Limitazione numero pagamenti effettivi  ---*
           if  L-TIPOCALCOLO   =  'R'
           then
               if  CTR-PAGATE  >  5999
               then
                   perform  DATICOMUNI-DB2-CLSCUR
                      thru  DATICOMUNI-DB2-CLSCUR-EX
                   move  'N'         to  WL-DATICOMUNI
                   move  'S'         to  W-FINE-INTERVALLO
                   perform  E60-SINCRONIZZO  thru  E60-EX
                   go to  E00-EX
               end-if
300320     end-if.
      *
           PERFORM  B20-DB2-FETCH    THRU  B20-DB2-FETCH-EX.
           IF SQLCODE = 0
               move  'S'         to  WL-DATICOMUNI
               move  H-DCOANVEPR to  WIC-ANNO
               move  H-DCONDVEPR to  WIC-NUMERO
               add  1            to  CTR-LET-DATCO
                                     CTR-VIDEO
           ELSE
               PERFORM DATICOMUNI-DB2-CLSCUR
                  THRU DATICOMUNI-DB2-CLSCUR-EX
               move  'N'         to  WL-DATICOMUNI
               move  'S'         to  W-FINE-INTERVALLO
               perform  E60-SINCRONIZZO  thru  E60-EX
           END-IF.
       E00-EX.
           exit.
      *
       E15-INIZIALIZZO.
           initialize    DSPFM13B-O.
           initialize    IC-AREA
                         OC-AREA.
           initialize    W-ANAGRAFICI
                         W-FST-SIINI
                         W-INIZIALIZZA
                         W-CONVERSIONI
                         W-STAMPAD.
           initialize    DCLTDSDATCO
                         DCLTDSRECUP
                         DCLTDSPEERE
                         DCLTDSAPIO0
                         DCLTDSDATAN
                         DCLTDSDELSI
                         DCLTDSMODAN
                         DCLTDSSOSPE
                         DCLTDSASU
                         DCLTDSASU2
                         DCLTDSLIST
                         DCLTDSLAV
                         DCLTDSPAG
                         DCLTDSATTSU
                         DCLTDSLAVPU
                         DCLTDSSUSST
                         DCLTDSPERIO.
      *
           move  'Y'     to  W-XCALCOLO.
           move  'N'     to  WL-RECUPERI
                             WL-FILE40
                             WL-FILE42
                             WL-FILE51
                             WL-FILE52
                             WL-FILE53
      *                      WL-FILE65
                             WL-SITUAZIODO.
           move  'N'     to  WS-APPOGGIO.
           move  spaces  to  W-CHK-CAMPI.
       E15-EX.
           exit.

       E20-ELABORA20.
      *--------- RIVEDERE
      *    Inserisci gestione domande definite con soli ANF
      *    da pagare: codice 'K' ??!
      *------------------------------------------ Compresa ?
           if  WIC-DOMANDA    <  W-DOMANDA-DAL
           then
      *-anno<>anno1 --------------------------------------
             if  TIPO-ELABO-IN   =  1            and
                 H-DCOANVEPR = ANNO-DAL-IN-LK(1)
                 go  to  E20-EX
             end-if
           end-if.
      *    if  WIC-DOMANDA    <  W-DOMANDA-DAL
      *    then
      *        go  to  E20-EX
      *    end-if
      *------------------------------------------ Codice struttura
           if H-DCOCENOPE                   is  numeric
           then
               continue
           else
               move

      *    move    ASUINI OF DCLTDSASU2        to  IC-ASUINID.
           MOVE    ASUINI OF DCLTDSASU2     TO  WK-DATA-APPOGGIO.

      *    move    ASUFIN OF DCLTDSASU2        to  IC-ASUFIND.

      *
           MOVE    PAGFINOA OF DCLTDSASU2   TO  WK-DATA-APPOGGIO.
           PERFORM CAMBIADATA-DA10-A8   THRU CAMBIADATA-DA10-A8-EX.
           if W8-AAAAMMGG = 99991231 or
              W8-AAAAMMGG = 00010101
              MOVE    0                 TO  IC-PAGFINOA
           else
              MOVE    W8-AAAAMMGG       TO  IC-PAGFINOA
           end-if.

           move    FLAGELAB OF DCLTDSASU2        to  IC-FLAGELAB.

      *

           MOVE    W8-AAAAMMGG              TO  IC-DATAREND.

       L72-CARICOPER.
           if  I-PER  <  50
           then
               add   1    to  I-PER
               move  H-PERDADAL      to  IC-PERDADAL(I-PER)
               move  H-PERDAAL       to  IC-PERDAAL(I-PER)
               move  H-PERCODICE     to  IC-PERCODICE(I-PER)
               if  H-PERCODICE =  17
               then
                   move  'S'  to  FLG-17
               end-if
               move  H-PERORELAV     to  IC-PERORELAV(I-PER)
           else
               move
                   'Stabellamento per elementi ADSPERIO               '
                             to  W-CHK-CAMPI
               move  'S'     to  W-ERRORE
               PERFORM TDSPERIO-DB2-CLSCUR
                  THRU TDSPERIO-DB2-CLSCUR-EX
               move  111     to  I-PER
           end-if.
       L72-EX.

               go  to  L73-EX

      *
       L75-TIPOASU.
      *--------------------------------------- Non alterare sequenza *
      *---- Le opzioni 4,5,6 sono state accorpate nella '4'          *
      *--------  '1-ASU Fondo Occupazione   Tipo fin. 3,6  (B)'      *
           if  (H-DCODTDECSP                  >   20000430)  and
               (H-ASUFIN                      =  3  or  6   or   9 )
           then
               move  '1'     to  W-OPZIONE
               go  to  L75-EX
           end-if.
      *--------  '2-ASU convenzione Enti    Tipo fin. 2    (B)'      *
           if  (H-DCODTDECSP                  >   20000430)  and
               (H-ASUFIN                      =  2)
           then
               move  '2'     to  W-OPZIONE
               go  to  L75-EX
           end-if.
      *--------  '3-Transitoristi ex F.O.   Tipo fin. 7    (B)'      *
           if  (H-DCODTDECSP                  >   20000430)  and
               (H-ASUFIN                      =  7)
           then
               move  '3'     to  W-OPZIONE
               go  to  L75-EX
           end-if.
      *--------  '4-ASU F.O. fino  31/10/00 Tipo fin.1     (B)'      *
           if  (H-DCODTDECSP                  <=  20001031)  and
               (H-ASUFIN                      =  1)
           then
               move  '4'     to  W-OPZIONE
               go  to  L75-EX
           end-if.
      *--------  '4-ASU F.O. fino  31/10/00 Tipo fin.1,4,5 (B)'      *
           if  (H-ASUFIN                      =  1  or  4  or  5)
           then

311017*------------------- Verifica altri pagamenti stesso giorno    *
           move  OC-CFENTEP     to  CODFIS     of  DCLTDSPAG.
           move  OC-ANNODELIBP  to  ANNODEL    of  DCLTDSPAG.
           move  OC-NUMDELIBP   to  NUMDEL     of  DCLTDSPAG.
           move  IC-DCOCODFIS   to  CFLAV      of  DCLTDSPAG.
           move  L-CODICE-SEDE  to  CODSAP     of  DCLTDSPAG.
           move  zeros             to  WK-DATA-APPOGGIO
                                       W8-AAAAMMGG .
           MOVE  OC-DATAPAGP       TO  W8-AAAAMMGG .
           PERFORM CAMBIADATA-DA8-A10  THRU  CAMBIADATA-DA8-A10-EX.
           MOVE  WK-DATA-APPOGGIO  TO  DATULT   OF DCLTDSPAG.
           move  zeros  to  W-CONTA-P.
      *
           EXEC SQL
             SELECT    COUNT(*)
             INTO      :W-CONTA-P
               FROM  TDSPAG
               WHERE  CODFIS     =  :DCLTDSPAG.CODFIS
                 AND  ANNODEL    =  :DCLTDSPAG.ANNODEL
                 AND  NUMDEL     =  :DCLTDSPAG.NUMDEL
                 AND  CFLAV      =  :DCLTDSPAG.CFLAV
                 AND  CODSAP     =  :DCLTDSPAG.CODSAP
                 AND  DATULT     =  :DCLTDSPAG.DATULT
           END-EXEC.
      *
           if  W-CONTA-P  >  0   or    SQLCODE  not =  zero
           then
               move  96  to  OC-RETCODE
               string
               'Avviso:   Prestazione non  pagabile oggi ma da'
               ' Domani in poi.         ' delimited by size
                   into  OC-MESSAGGIO
               go  to  E25-EX
311017     end-if.

           end-if.
      *-------------------------------------- Scrivo   EFFEROGATI    *
           if  (W-CODICEDUE    =  '42'       or
                W-CODICEDUE    =  '45')      and
      *         OC-DCOULESSP   =  'D'
      * 09/05/2018
               (OC-DCOULESSP   =  'D'        or
                IC-SSTCODIND       =  'CRED' or
                IC-SSTCODIND       =  'FTAD' or
270324          IC-SSTCODIND       =  'FSAD' or
                IC-SSTCODIND       =  'FTMD')

           end-if.
      *-------------------------------------- Riscrivo Assegno ASU   *
           if  W-CODICEDUE    =  '42'   and
               WL-FILE51      =  'S'
           then
               perform  E51-UPD-FILE51         thru  E51-EX
      *        if  (IC-ASUCFENTE   not  =  zeros)   and
      *            (IC-ASUANNODEL  not  =  zeros)   and
      *            (IC-ASUNUMDEL   not  =  zeros)
               if  (OC-CFENTEP     not  =  zeros)   and
                   (OC-ANNODELIBP  not  =  zeros)   and
                   (OC-NUMDELIBP   not  =  zeros)
100419       and
                   (OC-IMPASUF  >  0   or
                    OC-IMPANFF  >  0   or
                    OC-IMPMATF  >  0   or
                    OC-IMPASUE  >  0   or
                    OC-IMPANFE  >  0   or
100419              OC-IMPMATE  >  0 )

                   perform  E48-UPD-FILE48     thru  E48-EX
                   perform  E49-UPD-FILE49     thru  E49-EX
               end-if
           end-if.

           if  W-CODICEDUE    =  '45'   and
               WL-FILE53      =  'S'

      *        if  (OC-CODFIS         >  zeros)    and
      *            (OC-NOMEENTE  not  =  spaces)
               if  (OC-CFENTEP     not  =  zeros)   and
                   (OC-ANNODELIBP  not  =  zeros)   and
                   (OC-NUMDELIBP   not  =  zeros)

                   perform  E40-UPD-FILE40     thru  E40-EX
                   perform  E42-UPD-FILE42     thru  E42-EX

                   perform  E48-UPD-FILE48     thru  E48-EX
                   perform  E49-UPD-FILE49     thru  E49-EX
               end-if
           end-if.
      *-------------------------------------- Scrivo storico ANF     *
           if  IC-ANFDTDEVA(1)  >  zeros

GGA001*    move  IC-CFPRINC     to  CFPRINC    OF DCLTDSASU.
GGA001*    move  IC-NOMEFIN     to  NOMEFIN    OF DCLTDSASU.

       E43-UPD-RECUPERI.
           if  OC-RECIMUREE-1  =  zeroes   and

           move  IC-DCOCHIDOM  to H-RECCHIDOM .
           move  zeros         to H-RECPROREC .
      *
           PERFORM  E43-DB2-DECL-CURS    THRU  E43-DB2-DECL-CURS-EX.
      *
           move  zeros  to  NDC2.
           perform  varying  NDC1  from  1  by  1
                      until  NDC1  >  99
      *
            PERFORM  E43-DB2-FETCH    THRU  E43-DB2-FETCH-EX

            IF SQLCODE =    0
               move  'S'         to  WL-TABPIENA
               if  H-RECCHIDOM     is  equal IC-DCOCHIDOM
               then
                   perform E44-UPD-IMPORTI    thru E44-EX
                   if  OC-RECIMUREE-1  =  zeroes   and
                       OC-RECIMUREE-2  =  zeroes   and
                       OC-RECIMUREE-3  =  zeroes
                   then
                       PERFORM                                          CUR4
                          REC43-DB2-CLSCUR THRU REC43-DB2-CLSCUR-EX     CUR4
                       move  111    to  NDC1
                   end-if
               else
                   PERFORM                                              CUR4
                       REC43-DB2-CLSCUR THRU REC43-DB2-CLSCUR-EX        CUR4
                       move  111    to  NDC1
               end-if

             ELSE
               PERFORM                                                  CUR4
                   REC43-DB2-CLSCUR THRU REC43-DB2-CLSCUR-EX            CUR4
               move  111    to  NDC1
             END-IF
           end-perform.
      *------------------------------------- per i recuperi migrati  *
           if  OC-RECIMUREE-1  <  0.0100
           then
               move  zeroes   to  OC-RECIMUREE-1

           then

           end-if.
           if  OC-RECIMUREE-3  <  0.0100
           then

           end-if.
      *------------------------------------------------ a regime     *
           if  OC-RECIMUREE-1  =  zeroes   and
               OC-RECIMUREE-2  =  zeroes   and
               OC-RECIMUREE-3  =  zeroes

               continue
           else

               move  'KO-START  '       to  S2A005
               move  'ADSRECUP  '       to  S2A006
               move  FST-ADSRECUP       to  S2A007

            end-if.
           IF WL-TABPIENA = 'N'

       E44-UPD-IMPORTI.
           if  H-RECTORERE                 =  zeroes
           then
               go  to  E44-EX
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Recuperi Indennità  *
           if  OC-RECIMUREE-1  >  zeroes
           then
               if  (H-RECCAUREC                =  '1')   and
                   (H-RECTIPREC                =  'R')
               then
                   if  H-RECTORERE                =  OC-RECIMUREE-1
                   then
                       move  W8-ODIERNA  to H-RECDTESRE
                       move  OC-RECIMUREE-1
                                         to H-RECIMUREE
                       move  zeroes      to H-RECTORERE
                       move  zeroes      to  OC-RECIMUREE-1
                   end-if
                   if  H-RECTORERE                >  OC-RECIMUREE-1
                   then
                       move  W8-ODIERNA  to H-RECDTESRE
                       move  OC-RECIMUREE-1
                                         to H-RECIMUREE
                       subtract  OC-RECIMUREE-1
                                       from H-RECTORERE
                       move  zeroes      to  OC-RECIMUREE-1
                   end-if
                   if  H-RECTORERE                <  OC-RECIMUREE-1
                   then
                       move  W8-ODIERNA  to H-RECDTESRE
                       move H-RECTORERE
                                         to H-RECIMUREE
                       subtract H-RECTORERE
                                       from  OC-RECIMUREE-1
                       move  zeroes      to H-RECTORERE
                   end-if
               end-if
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Recuperi/acconti ANF*
           if  OC-RECIMUREE-2  >  zeroes
           then
               if  H-RECCAUREC                =  '2'
               then
                   if  H-RECTORERE                =  OC-RECIMUREE-2
                   then
                       move  W8-ODIERNA  to H-RECDTESRE
                       move  OC-RECIMUREE-2
                                         to H-RECIMUREE
                       move  zeroes      to H-RECTORERE
                       move  zeroes      to  OC-RECIMUREE-2
                   end-if
                   if  H-RECTORERE                >  OC-RECIMUREE-2
                   then
                       move  W8-ODIERNA  to H-RECDTESRE
                       move  OC-RECIMUREE-2
                                         to H-RECIMUREE
                       subtract  OC-RECIMUREE-2
                                       from H-RECTORERE
                       move  zeroes      to  OC-RECIMUREE-2
                   end-if
                   if  H-RECTORERE                <  OC-RECIMUREE-2
                   then
                       move  W8-ODIERNA  to H-RECDTESRE
                       move H-RECTORERE
                                         to H-RECIMUREE
                       subtract H-RECTORERE
                                       from  OC-RECIMUREE-2
                       move  zeroes      to H-RECTORERE
                   end-if
               end-if
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Acconto indennità   *
           if  OC-RECIMUREE-3  >  zeroes
           then
      *        if  H-RECTIPREC                =  'A'
               if  (H-RECCAUREC  =  "1")   and
                   (H-RECTIPREC  =  "A")
               then
                   if  H-RECTORERE                =  OC-RECIMUREE-3
                   then
                       move  W8-ODIERNA  to H-RECDTESRE
                       move  OC-RECIMUREE-3
                                         to H-RECIMUREE
                       move  zeroes      to H-RECTORERE
                       move  zeroes      to  OC-RECIMUREE-3
                   end-if
                   if  H-RECTORERE                >  OC-RECIMUREE-3
                   then
                       move  W8-ODIERNA  to H-RECDTESRE
                       move  OC-RECIMUREE-3
                                         to H-RECIMUREE
                       subtract  OC-RECIMUREE-3
                                       from H-RECTORERE
                       move  zeroes      to  OC-RECIMUREE-3
                   end-if
                   if  H-RECTORERE                <  OC-RECIMUREE-3
                   then
                       move  W8-ODIERNA  to H-RECDTESRE
                       move H-RECTORERE
                                         to H-RECIMUREE

                                       from  OC-RECIMUREE-3

           move  OC-CFENTEP     to  CODFIS  OF DCLTDSPAG.

           PERFORM CAMBIADATA-DA8-A10 THRU CAMBIADATA-DA8-A10-EX.

           move  IC-CODSEDE     to  CODSAP  OF DCLTDSPAG.
      *    move  OC-DATAPAGP    to  DATULT   OF DCLTDSPAG.
           MOVE  OC-DATAPAGP    TO   W8-AAAAMMGG .
           PERFORM CAMBIADATA-DA8-A10 THRU CAMBIADATA-DA8-A10-EX.
           MOVE    WK-DATA-APPOGGIO    TO DATULT   OF DCLTDSPAG.
           move  OC-IMPASUF     to  ASUFONDO OF DCLTDSPAG.
           compute ASUFONDO OF DCLTDSPAG =
                   ASUFONDO OF DCLTDSPAG * 0.01.
           move  OC-IMPANFF     to  ANFFONDO OF DCLTDSPAG.
           compute ANFFONDO OF DCLTDSPAG =
                   ANFFONDO OF DCLTDSPAG * 0.01.
           move  OC-IMPMATF     to  MATFONDO OF DCLTDSPAG.
           compute MATFONDO OF DCLTDSPAG =
                   MATFONDO OF DCLTDSPAG * 0.01.
           move  OC-IMPASUE     to  ASUENTE OF DCLTDSPAG.
           compute ASUENTE  OF DCLTDSPAG =
                   ASUENTE  OF DCLTDSPAG * 0.01.
           move  OC-IMPANFE     to  ANFENTE OF DCLTDSPAG.
           compute ANFENTE  OF DCLTDSPAG =
                   ANFENTE  OF DCLTDSPAG * 0.01.
           move  OC-IMPMATE     to  MATENTE OF DCLTDSPAG.
           compute MATENTE  OF DCLTDSPAG =
                   MATENTE  OF DCLTDSPAG * 0.01.
      *
           move  OC-COD1        to  CODPER1         .
      *
           if    OC-DATADAL1 > 0
           then
               MOVE  OC-DATADAL1          TO   W8-AAAAMMGG
               PERFORM CAMBIADATA-DA8-A10 THRU CAMBIADATA-DA8-A10-EX
               MOVE    WK-DATA-APPOGGIO   TO   DATDAL1

               MOVE    WK-DATA-APPOGGIO   TO   DATAL1
           ELSE
               MOVE '01.01.0001'          TO   DATDAL1 DATAL1
           END-IF.
      *

      *
           if    OC-DATADAL2 > 0

       E55-WRT-STOANF.
           move  'N'  to  LC-RETCODE.
      *
           call  PDSPD04 using
                        WDFHEIBLK  WDFHCOMMAREA
                                   L-CODICE-SEDE
                                   W-PROCEDURA
                                   L-CODICE-STOP
                                   W8-ODIERNA
                                   IC-DOMANDA
                                   W-PROGRESSIVO
                                   IC-DCOCODFIS
                                   IC-DCOCHIDOM
      *I------------------------------- new dal 23/07/2013           *
      *                            IC-TAB-ANF
                                   LC-TAB-ANF
      *F------------------------------- new dal 23/07/2013           *
                                   LC-RETCODE
           end-call.
           cancel  PDSPD04 .
       E55-EX.
           EXIT.
      *
       E56-WRT-STOSOS.
           move  'N'  to  LC-RETCODE.
      *
           call  PDSPD06     USING
                           WDFHEIBLK  WDFHCOMMAREA
                                   L-CODICE-SEDE
                                   W-PROCEDURA
                                   L-CODICE-STOP
                                   W8-ODIERNA
                                   IC-DOMANDA
                                   W-PROGRESSIVO
                                   IC-DCOCODFIS
                                   IC-DCOCHIDOM
                                   IC-TAB-SOSPE
                                   LC-RETCODE
           end-call.
           cancel  PDSPD06 .
       E56-EX.
           EXIT.
      *
       E60-SINCRONIZZO.
      *----------------------------------- Lista controllo
           if  L-TIPOCALCOLO  =  'S'
           then
 GGAS *    EXEC CICS
 GGAS *       SYNCPOINT  ROLLBACK
 GGAS *    END-EXEC
               if  W-FINE-ELABORA  =  'S' and TIPO-ELABO-IN < '3'
               then
               if  CTR-PAGATE  >  zeros OR CTR-INDEBITE >  zeros
               then
      *            EXEC CICS SYNCPOINT  ROLLBACK END-EXEC
                   perform  S40-IMPOSTAZIONI  thru  S40-EX
      *            MOVE S5A000       TO R5A000
                   MOVE S5N001       TO R5N001
      *            MOVE S5A002       TO R5A002
      *            MOVE S5A003       TO R5A003
                   MOVE S5N004       TO R5N004
                   MOVE S5N005       TO R5N005
                   MOVE S5N007       TO R5N007
                   MOVE S5N006       TO R5N006
                   MOVE S5N008       TO R5N008
                   MOVE S5N009       TO R5N009
                   MOVE S5N011       TO R5N011
                   MOVE S5N012       TO R5N012
      *            perform  S40-IMPOSTAZIONI  thru  S40-EX
                   MOVE R-STAMPAS    TO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
                   MOVE  0           TO TDSREPORT-NUM-RIGA
      *
           PERFORM S30-INSERT-REPORT THRU S30-EX-INSERT-REPORT
      *
               else
                   MOVE 'NESSUNA DOMANDA DA PAGARE' TO  OUT-MESSAGGIO
                   move  '96'           to  OUT-STATUS
               end-if
               end-if
               go  to  E60-EX
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------- Fine Calcolo reale
           if  W-FINE-ELABORA     =  'S'
           then
               if  CTR-PAGATE   >  zeros   or
                   CTR-DEFINITE >  zeros
               then
      ********* ELABORAZIONE TERMINATA *****
                   perform  S40-IMPOSTAZIONI  thru  S40-EX
                   MOVE R-STAMPAS    TO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT
                   MOVE  0           TO TDSREPORT-NUM-RIGA
      *
           PERFORM S30-INSERT-REPORT THRU S30-EX-INSERT-REPORT
               else
                   perform  S40-IMPOSTAZIONI  thru  S40-EX
                EXEC CICS
                   SYNCPOINT  ROLLBACK
                END-EXEC
      ********* ELABORAZIONE TERMINATA *****
                   MOVE 'NESSUNA DOMANDA DA PAGARE' TO  OUT-MESSAGGIO
                   move  '96'           to  OUT-STATUS
                   go  to  E60-EX
               end-if
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------- Impostazione Riepilogo
           if  (CTR-PAGATE  >  zeros      or
                CTR-DEFINITE  >  zeros)   and
               (FLG-COMMIT  =  'S')
           then
               if  WS-RIEPILOGO  =  'N'
               then
                   perform  E62-SCRIVO         thru  E62-EX
               else
                   perform  E64-RISCRIVO       thru  E64-EX
               end-if
           end-if.
      *-------------------------------------- Sincronia intermedia
           if  WS-APPOGGIO  =  'S'
           then  continue
           else
      *          perform E60-POP      thru  E60-POP-EX
                 go  to  E60-EX
           end-if.

           if  CTR-PAGATE    >  zeros    or
               CTR-DEFINITE  >  zeros
           then
               if  FLG-COMMIT  =  'S'
               then
                  EXEC CICS
                   SYNCPOINT
                  END-EXEC
                   move  'N'    to  FLG-COMMIT
               else
              EXEC CICS
                   SYNCPOINT  ROLLBACK
              END-EXEC
      *            subtract  1           from  CTR-SCR-APPO
                   move  WIC-DOMANDA       to  W-DOMANDA-DAL
                   add   1                 to  W-DOMANDA-DAL
                   perform  B20-PERSTART  thru  B20-EX
               end-if
           end-if.
       E60-EX.
           EXIT.
      *
       E60-POP.
      *
      *----- GESTIONE ANNULLAMENTO RECUPERO IN CASO DI ABEND.
      *
      *     IF OC-FCODPAGA1    = '730'
           IF OC-CODICE2    = '730'
              initialize  area-input-in
              MOVE ZEROES           TO REC-IMPORTO-MASSIMO-IN
              MOVE SPACES           TO REC-NUMERO-PRATICA-IN
              MOVE ZEROES           TO REC-PROGRESSIVO-PRATICA-IN
              MOVE SPACES           TO REC-CHIAVE-RESTART-IN
              MOVE SPACES           TO REC-UTENZA
              MOVE ZEROES           TO REC-DATA-IN
              move W8-ODIERNA       to REC-DATA-IN
              MOVE REC-DATA-IN(5:2) to REC-RATA-IN
              MOVE REC-DATA-IN(1:4) to REC-ANNO-IN
              move L-CODICE-SEDE    to REC-SEDE-IN
              move L-CODICE-STOP    to REC-SEDE-IN(5:2)
              MOVE '035'            TO TIPO-RICHIESTA-IN-5
              MOVE 'G05'            TO REC-PROCEDURA-CHIAMANTE-IN
              MOVE IC-CODFISARCA    TO REC-CODICE-FISCALE-IN
      *       MOVE OC-FIMPPAGA1     TO REC-IMPORTO-TRATTATO-IN
              MOVE OC-IMPORTO2      TO REC-IMPORTO-TRATTATO-IN
              MOVE  '999999'        TO RETCODE-00
      *
              EXEC CICS LINK PROGRAM(POPWMAIN)                          03050003
                             COMMAREA(AREA-POPSIN)                      03050003
              END-EXEC                                                  03050003
      *
              IF RETCODE-00 not = '000000'
                 display  'POP RETCODE =' RETCODE-00 '-' H-DCOCHIDOM
                           '--' area-input-in(1:100)
              ELSE
                 display  'POP ANNULLATO RECUPERO =' H-DCOCHIDOM
                           '--' area-input-in(1:100)
              END-IF
           END-IF.
       E60-POP-EX.
           EXIT.

       E62-SCRIVO.
           initialize  DCLTDSRPG00.
      *----------------------------------- Impostazione key          *
           move  W8-ODIERNA     to  H-PDATAELABO.
           move  W-PROGRESSIVO  to  H-PPROGRESSI.
           move  W-PROCEDURA    to  H-PPROCEDURA.
           move  L-CODICE-STOP  to  H-PSTRUTTURA.
           move  L-CODICE-SEDE  to  H-PCOSEDE.
      *----------------------------------- Errore per lettura valida *
           PERFORM E62-DB2-SELECT THRU E62-DB2-SELECT-EX.
      *
           IF  SQLCODE = 0
                 move   7      to  NDT2
                 move  zeros   to  CTR-PAGATE
                 move  'S'     to  W-FINE-INTERVALLO
                 go  to  E62-EX
           end-IF.
      *----------------------------------- Impostazione dati         *
           move  'N'           to  H-PBACKUP.
           move  W8-ODIERNA    to  W8-AAAAMMGG.
           if  W8-MM     >  1
           then
               subtract     1   from  W8-MM
           else
               move  12           to  W8-MM
               subtract     1   from  W8-AAAA
           end-if.
           if  W8-MM     =  04   or  =  06   or  =  09   or  =  11
           then
               move  30           to  W8-GG
           else
               if  W8-MM     =  02
               then
                   move  28           to  W8-GG
               else
                   move  31           to  W8-GG
               end-if
           end-if.
           move  W8-AAAAMMGG      to  H-PCALCOLOAL.
           move  CTR-SCR-APPO     to  H-PCALCOLATI.
           move  zeroes           to  H-PRECPAGATI.
           move  'N'              to  H-PFINEPAGAM.
           if  CTR-PAGATE  >  zeros
           then
               move  " "          to  H-PZEROPAGAM
           else
               if  CTR-DEFINITE  >  zeros
               then
                   move  "S"      to  H-PZEROPAGAM
               end-if
           end-if.
           move  zeroes           to  H-PIMPCONTAB
                                      H-PIMPTELEMA.
           move  spaces           to  H-PCODTELEMA.
           move  zeroes           to  H-PDATAEMISS.
           move  W-PAGARE         to  H-PCHEDOMAND.
           move  X1-CHEPRESTA     to  H-PCHEPRESTA.
           move  PERIODI-IN-LK    to  H-PCHENUMERA.
      *    move  T2-INTERVALLI    to  H-PCHENUMERA.
      *
           PERFORM E62-DB2-INSERT THRU E62-DB2-INSERT-EX.
      *
           IF  SQLCODE NOT = 0
                 move  'WRITE     '   to  S2A005
                 move  'ADSRPG00  '   to  S2A006
                 move  FST-ADSRPG00   to  S2A007
                 perform  S10-STAMPA  thru  S10-EX
                 move   7             to  NDT2
                 move  zeros          to  CTR-PAGATE
                 move  'S'            to  W-FINE-INTERVALLO
                 go  to  E62-EX
           ELSE
                 move  'S'            to  WS-RIEPILOGO
                 continue
           end-IF.
       E62-EX.
           EXIT.
      *
       E64-RISCRIVO.
           move  CTR-SCR-APPO    to  H-PCALCOLATI.
      *
           if  CTR-PAGATE  >  zeros
           then
               move  ' '          to  H-PZEROPAGAM
           else
               if  CTR-DEFINITE  >  zeros
               then
                   move  'S'      to  H-PZEROPAGAM
               end-if
           end-if.
      *
           PERFORM E64-DB2-UPDATE THRU E64-DB2-UPDATE-EX.
      *
           IF  SQLCODE NOT = 0
                 move  'REWRITE   '       to  S2A005
                 move  'ADSRPG00  '       to  S2A006
                 move  FST-ADSRPG00       to  S2A007
                 perform  S10-STAMPA     thru  S10-EX
                 perform  T13-TESTO13    thru  T13-EX
                 perform  W10-MSGERRORE  thru  W10-EX
                 move   7                 to  NDT2
                 move  zeros              to  CTR-PAGATE
                 move  'S'                to  W-FINE-INTERVALLO
                 go  to  E64-EX
           end-IF.
       E64-EX.
           EXIT.
      *
       F00-FINALI.
           if  W-FLAGYNCORSO  =  'S'
           then
               perform F20-FINYNCORSO   thru  F20-EX
           end-if.
      *
           if  (K-RETURN-CODE   not  =  'KO')  and

           perform  J12-QUADRAFISCO    thru  J12-EX.
           if  W-ERRORE  =  'S'
           then
               go  to  J10-EX
           end-if.
      *---------------------------------------- Solo per ....        *
           if  OC-FADNETTOPAG  >  zeroes
           then
               continue
           else
               go  to  J10-EX
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Verifica
           move  zeros             to  W-DIFFERENZA.
           compute  W-DIFFERENZA    =  OC-FACIMPONIBILE
                                    -  OC-FACIMPNETTA
                                    +  OC-FACTREDICESIMA
                                    +  OC-FAPTREDICESIMA
                                    +  OC-FAPIMPONIBILE
                                    -  OC-FAPIMPNETTA
                                    +  OC-FADANFPAGATI
      *                             -  OC-FADRECSUIND
      *                             -  OC-FADRECSUANF
                                    -  OC-FADTRATSIND
                                    -  OC-FCONGAC
                                    -  OC-FCONGAP
                                    -  OC-FIMPREGAC
                                    -  OC-FIMPREGAP
                                    -  OC-FIMPCOMAC
                                    -  OC-FIMPCOMAP
                                    -  OC-FADNETTOPAG.
      *
           if  OC-FCODPAGA1  =  'ACC'
           then
               subtract  OC-FIMPPAGA1
                                 from  W-DIFFERENZA
           end-if.
      *    if  OC-FCODPAGA1  =  '730'
           if  OC-CODICE2    =  '730'
           then
      *        subtract  OC-FIMPPAGA1
               subtract  OC-IMPORTO2
                                 from  W-DIFFERENZA
           end-if.
           if  OC-FCODPAGA1  =  'SNI'
           then
               add       OC-FIMPPAGA1
                                  to   W-DIFFERENZA
           end-if.
           move  W-DIFFERENZA      to  W-SQUADRATURA.
           if  W-DIFFERENZA  =  zeros
           then
               continue
           else
               move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
               go  to  J10-EX
           end-if.
      *-------------------------------------------------------
           if  OC-DCOULESSP   equal  spaces
           then
               move  'Campo OC-DCOULESSP    non impostato             '
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
               move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
               go  to  J10-EX
           end-if.
           if  OC-FADINIZIO   equal  zeros
           then
               move  'Campo OC-FADINIZIO  non impostato               '
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
               move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
               go  to  J10-EX
           end-if.
           if  OC-FADFINE    equal  zeros
           then
               move  'Campo OC-FADFINE    non impostato               '
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
               move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
               go  to  J10-EX
           end-if.
      *    if  OC-PMEUITRSIE  =  OC-FADTRATSIND
      *    then
      *        continue
      *    else
      *        move  'Valore di OC-PMEUITRSIE  non = OC-FADTRATSIND   '
      *                                              to  W-CHK-CAMPI
      *        move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
      *        go  to  J10-EX
      *    end-if.
      *    if  (OC-PMEINDUIME     +  OC-PMEINLEPRE)  equal
      *        (OC-FACIMPONIBILE  +  OC-FAPIMPONIBILE)
      *    then
      *        continue
      *    else
      *        move  'OC-PME(INDUIME+INLEPRE) not= OC(FAC+FAPIMPONIBIL'
      *                                              to  W-CHK-CAMPI
      *        move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
      *        go  to  J10-EX
      *    end-if.
      *    if  (OC-PMEANFUIME     +  OC-PMEINLEANE)  equal
      *        OC-FADANFPAGATI
      *    then
      *        continue
      *    else
      *        move  'OC-PME(ANFUIME+INLEANE) not= OC-FADANFPAGATI    '
      *                                              to  W-CHK-CAMPI
      *        move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
      *        go  to  J10-EX
      *    end-if.
      *------------------------------------ Pagamento solo ANF?      *
           if  OC-FACIMPONIBILE  =  zeros   and
               OC-FACTREDICESIMA =  zeros   and
               OC-FAPIMPONIBILE  =  zeros   and
               OC-FAPTREDICESIMA =  zeros
           then
               if  OC-FADANFPAGATI  >  zeroes
               then
                   go  to  J10-EX
               end-if
           end-if.
      *
      *    if  OC-FACGGPREST  >  zeros   or
      *        OC-FAPGGPREST  >  zeros   or
      *        OC-CODICE1     =  'G11'
      *    then
      *        continue
      *    else
      *        if  OC-ASUIMRINU   =  zeros
      *        and OC-FADNETTOPAG =  zeros
      *        then
      *            move
      *              'OC-FACGGPREST and OC-FAPGGPREST = zero          '
      *                                              to  W-CHK-CAMPI
      *            move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
      *            go  to  J10-EX
      *        else
      *            continue
      *        end-if
      *    end-if.
      *    if  OC-FACGGDETRAZ  >  zeros   or
      *        OC-FAPGGDETRAZ  >  zeros   or
      *        OC-CODICE1     =  'G11'
      *    then
      *        continue
      *    else
      *        if   OC-ASUIMRINU   =  zeros
      *        and  OC-SSTIMRINU   =  zeros
      *        and  OC-SSTIMINU    =  zeros
      *        and OC-FADNETTOPAG =  zeros
      *        then
      *            move
      *              'OC-FACGGDETRAZ and OC-FAPGGDETRAZ = zero        '
      *                                              to  W-CHK-CAMPI
      *            move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
      *            go  to  J10-EX
      *        else
      *            continue
      *        end-if
      *    end-if.
      *    if  (OC-RECIMUREE-1  +  OC-RECIMUREE-3)  equal
      *         OC-FADRECSUIND
      *    then
      *        continue
      *    else
      *        move  'OC-(RECIMUREE1+/RECIMUREE2) not= OC-FADRECSUIND'
      *                                              to  W-CHK-CAMPI
      *        move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
      *        go  to  J10-EX
      *    end-if.
      *    if   OC-RECIMUREE-2  equal
      *         OC-FADRECSUANF
      *    then
      *        continue
      *    else
      *        move  'OC-RECIMUREE-2 not= OC-FADRECSUANF             '
      *                                              to  W-CHK-CAMPI
      *        move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
      *        go  to  J10-EX
      *    end-if.
       J10-EX.
           EXIT.
      *
       J12-QUADRAFISCO.
           move  zeros             to  W-DIF-FISCALE.
      *    if  OC-FCODPAGA1  =  '730'  or
      *    if  OC-CODICE2    =  '730'  or
      *    if  OC-FCODPAGA1  =  'ACC'
      *    then
               compute  W-DIF-FISCALE   =
               ((OC-FACIMPONIBILE  +  OC-FACTREDICESIMA
                                   -  OC-FACIMPNETTA)      +
                (OC-FAPIMPONIBILE  +  OC-FAPTREDICESIMA
                                   -  OC-FAPIMPNETTA)      +
                (OC-FADANFPAGATI)                          -
                (OC-FADTRATSIND)                           -
                (OC-FCONGAC        +  OC-FCONGAP)          -
                (OC-FIMPREGAC      +  OC-FIMPREGAP)        -
                (OC-FIMPCOMAC      +  OC-FIMPCOMAP)        -
                 OC-FIMPPAGA1                              -
                 OC-IMPORTO2)                              -
                 OC-FADNETTOPAG.
      *    end-if.
      *
      *    if  OC-FCODPAGA1  =  '   '  or
           if  OC-FCODPAGA1  =  'SNI'
           then
               compute  W-DIF-FISCALE   =
               ((OC-FACIMPONIBILE  +  OC-FACTREDICESIMA
                                   -  OC-FACIMPNETTA)      +
                (OC-FAPIMPONIBILE  +  OC-FAPTREDICESIMA
                                   -  OC-FAPIMPNETTA)      +
                (OC-FADANFPAGATI)                          -
                (OC-FADTRATSIND)                           -
                (OC-FCONGAC        +  OC-FCONGAP)          -
                (OC-FIMPREGAC      +  OC-FIMPREGAP)        -
                (OC-FIMPCOMAC      +  OC-FIMPCOMAP)        +
                 OC-FIMPPAGA1                              -
                 OC-IMPORTO2)                              -
                 OC-FADNETTOPAG
           end-if.
      *
           if  W-DIF-FISCALE  =  zeros
           then
               continue
           else
               move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
               move
                 'Errore quadratura fiscale: segnala a  HELP-DSORD'
                                        to  W-CHK-CAMPI
      *        go  to  J12-EX
           end-if.
       J12-EX.
           EXIT.

       J20-MUOVIEURO.
      *----------------------------------------- Tipo prestazione    *
           if  W-CODICEDUE  =  42

           end-if.
           if  W-CODICEDUE  =  44

           end-if.
           if  W-CODICEDUE  =  45

           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Squadratura
           if  W-NIK  =  'S'
           then
               if  W-DIFFERENZA     =  zeros
               then
                   move  spaces     to  MBA041  of  VO-DSPFM13B
               else
                   string  'Att. squadra di euro '
                                        delimited   by  size
                      R-SQUADRATURA     delimited   by  size
                                  into  MBA041  of  VO-DSPFM13B
                   go  to  J20-EX
               end-if
               if  W-CHK-CAMPI       =  spaces
               then
                   move  spaces     to  MBA041  of  VO-DSPFM13B
               else
                   string  'ATT: '
                                        delimited   by  size
                      W-CHK-CAMPI       delimited   by  size
                                  into  MBA041  of  VO-DSPFM13B
               end-if
           end-if.
       J20-EX.
           EXIT.

       J22-ASUEURO.
      *----------------------------------------- Data riferim. calcol*
           move  OC-ASUULASS        to  W8-AAAAMMGG.

      *----------------------------------------- Totale indennita'
           move  OC-ASUIMINT         to  MBN014  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *     add  OC-ASUIMRIN         to  MBN014  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Totale gg. indenn.
           move  OC-ASUGGCALC        to  MBN015  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Totale ANF
           move  OC-ASUIMANFT        to  MBN017  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
            add  OC-ASUMAGANFT       to  MBN017  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Totale gg. ANF
      *    move  OC-???ANFTOGG       to  MBN018  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Totale tratt. IRPEF AC
      *    move  OC-???TOIRNCE       to  MBN020  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Totale tratt. IRPEF AP
      *    move  OC-???TOIRNPE       to  MBN030  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Totale tratt. sindac.
      *    move  OC-???TOTRSIE       to  MBN022  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Ultimo importo ind. *
           move  OC-ASUIMINU         to  MBN013  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
            add  OC-ASUIMRINU        to  MBN013  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
           if  MBN013  of  VO-DSPFM13B  >  zeros
           then
               if  OC-ASUIMINU   =
                              (OC-FACIMPONIBILE  +  OC-FAPIMPONIBILE)
               then
                   continue
               else
                   move
                     'OC-ASUIMINU not= OC-(FAC+FAPIMPONIBILE)         '
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
                   move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
               end-if
               if  OC-ASUIMRINU  =   OC-FACTREDICESIMA
               then
                   continue
               else
                   move
                     'OC-ASUIMRINU not= OC-FACTREDICESIMA             '
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
                   move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
               end-if
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Indebito?           *
           if  MBN013  of  VO-DSPFM13B  =  zeros
           then
               move  OC-ASUINDEB     to  MBN013  of  VO-DSPFM13B
               multiply  -1          by  MBN013  of  VO-DSPFM13B
           end-if.
      *    if  OC-ASUINDEB  >  zeros
      *    then
      *        if  OC-ASUINDEB   =
      *                       (OC-FACIMPONIBILE  +  OC-FAPIMPONIBILE)
      *        then
      *            continue
      *        else
      *            move
      *              'OC-ASUINDEB not= OC-(FAC+FAPIMPONIBILE)         '
      *                                              to  W-CHK-CAMPI
      *            move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
      *        end-if
      *    end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Ultimo importo ANF
           move  OC-ASUIMANFU        to  MBN016  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
            add  OC-ASUMAGANF        to  MBN016  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
           if  (OC-ASUIMANFU  +  OC-ASUMAGANF)  =  OC-FADANFPAGATI
           then
               continue
           else
               move  'OC-FADANFPAGATI not=  OC-(ASUIMANFU+ASUMAGANF)  '
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
               move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Ultima tratt. IRPEF AC
           move  OC-FACIMPNETTA      to  MBN019  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
           if  OC-ASUIRPEFU  =  OC-FACIMPNETTA  +  OC-FAPIMPNETTA

                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
               move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Ultima tratt. IRPEF AP
           move  OC-FAPIMPNETTA      to  MBN029  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Conguaglio Irpef AP
           if  OC-ASUCONGFIS  <  zeroes
           then
               string  'Rimborso   Irpef '   delimited  by  size
                       W4-ANNO-1             delimited  by  size
                                  into  MBA031  of  VO-DSPFM13B
               move  OC-ASUCONGFIS  to  MBN032  of  VO-DSPFM13B
           end-if.
           if  OC-ASUCONGFIS  >  zeroes
           then
               string  'Conguaglio Irpef '   delimited  by  size
                       W4-ANNO-1             delimited  by  size
                                  into  MBA031  of  VO-DSPFM13B
               move  OC-ASUCONGFIS  to  MBN032  of  VO-DSPFM13B
           end-if.
           if  OC-ASUCONGFIS  =  (OC-FCONGAC  +  OC-FCONGAP)

           else
               move  'OC-ASUCONGFIS not= OC-FCONGAC + OC-FCONGAP      '
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
               move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
           end-if.

           if  OC-ASUCONG730  not =  zeroes

                                    to  MBA031  of  VO-DSPFM13B

      *        if  OC-ASUCONG730  =   OC-FIMPPAGA1   and
      *            OC-FCODPAGA1   =   '730'

                   OC-CODICE2     =   '730'

      *        move  'OC-ASUCONG730 not= OC-FIMPPAGA1                 '
               move  'OC-ASUCONG730 not= OC-IMPORTO2                  '
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
                   move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
               end-if
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Addizionale Regionale
           move  OC-ASUADDIZR       to  MBN033  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
            add  OC-ASUADDIZRR      to  MBN033  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
           if  (OC-ASUADDIZR   +   OC-ASUADDIZRR)  =
                                 (OC-FIMPREGAC  +  OC-FIMPREGAP)

               move  'OC-ASUADDIZR  not= OC-(FIMPREGAC + FIMPREGAP)   '

               move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE

      *----------------------------------------- Addizionale Comunale
           move  OC-ASUADDIZC       to  MBN034  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
            add  OC-ASUADDIZRC      to  MBN034  of  VO-DSPFM13B.

      *----------------------------------------- Acconto
           move  OC-RECIMUREE-3      to  MBN023  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
           if  OC-FCODPAGA1    =  'ACC'
               if  OC-RECIMUREE-3  =  OC-FIMPPAGA1

                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
                   move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
               end-if
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Ultimo  recupero ind.
           move   OC-RECIMUREE-1     to  MBN024  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
            add   OC-ASURECRIN       to  MBN024  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
GG         if  OC-FADNETTOPAG > 0
           then
             if  OC-RECIMUREE-1  +  OC-ASURECRIN  =  OC-FADRECSUIND
             then
                continue
             else
                move  'OC-FADRECSUIND not= OC-RECIMUREE-1 + OC-ASURECRI'
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
                move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
             end-if
GG         end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Sommo recuperi      *
           add   OC-RECIMUREE-1      to  MBN013  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
           add   OC-ASURECRIN        to  MBN013  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Ultimo  recupero ANF
           add   OC-RECIMUREE-2      to  MBN024  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
           if  OC-FADRECSUANF  =  OC-RECIMUREE-2
           then

                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
               move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Sommo recuperi      *
           add   OC-RECIMUREE-2      to  MBN016  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Interessi indennità
      *    move  zeros               to  MBN025  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *    add   OC-***INLEPRE       to  MBN025  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Interessi ANF
      *    add   OC-***INLEANE       to  MBN025  of  VO-DSPFM13B.

      *----------------------------------------- Assegno

      *    if  OC-LPUINDEB  >  zeros
      *    then
      *        if  OC-LPUINDEB   =

            add  OC-LPUMAGANF        to  MBN016  of  VO-DSPFM13B.

      *----------------------------------------- Ultima tratt. IRPEF AC
           move  OC-FACIMPNETTA      to  MBN019  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
           if  OC-LPUIRPEFU  =  OC-FACIMPNETTA  +  OC-FAPIMPNETTA
           then
               continue
           else
               move  'OC-LPUIRPEFU not= OC-(FAC+FAPIMPNETTA)          '
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
               move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Ultima tratt. IRPEF AP
           move  OC-FAPIMPNETTA      to  MBN029  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Conguaglio Irpef AP
           if  OC-LPUCONGFIS  <  zeroes
           then
               string  'Rimborso   Irpef '   delimited  by  size
                       W4-ANNO-1             delimited  by  size
                                  into  MBA031  of  VO-DSPFM13B
               move  OC-LPUCONGFIS  to  MBN032  of  VO-DSPFM13B
           end-if.
           if  OC-LPUCONGFIS  >  zeroes
           then
               string  'Conguaglio Irpef '   delimited  by  size
                       W4-ANNO-1             delimited  by  size
                                  into  MBA031  of  VO-DSPFM13B
               move  OC-LPUCONGFIS  to  MBN032  of  VO-DSPFM13B
           end-if.
           if  OC-LPUCONGFIS  =  (OC-FCONGAC  +  OC-FCONGAP)
           then
               continue
           else
               move  'OC-LPUCONGFIS not= OC-FCONGAC + OC-FCONGAP      '
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
               move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Conguaglio Irpef 730
           if  OC-LPUCONG730  not =  zeroes
           then
               move  'Conguaglio da 730    '
                                    to  MBA031  of  VO-DSPFM13B
               move  OC-LPUCONG730  to  MBN032  of  VO-DSPFM13B
           end-if.
      *    if  OC-FCODPAGA1   =   '730'
           if  OC-CODICE2     =   '730'
           then
      *        if  OC-LPUCONG730  =   OC-FIMPPAGA1
               if  OC-LPUCONG730  =   OC-IMPORTO2
               then
                   continue
               else
                   move
      *              'OC-LPUCONG730 not= OC-FIMPPAGA1                 '
                     'OC-LPUCONG730 not= OC-IMPORTO2                  '
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
                   move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
               end-if
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Addizionale Regionale
           move  OC-LPUADDIZR       to  MBN033  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
           if  OC-LPUADDIZR   =  (OC-FIMPREGAC  +  OC-FIMPREGAP)
           then
               continue
           else
               move  'OC-LPUADDIZR  not= OC-(FIMPREGAC + FIMPREGAP)   '
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
               move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Addizionale Comunale
           move  OC-LPUADDIZC       to  MBN034  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
           if  OC-LPUADDIZC   =  (OC-FIMPCOMAC  +  OC-FIMPCOMAP)
           then
               continue
           else
               move  'OC-LPUADDIZC  not= OC-(FIMPCOMAC + FIMPCOMAP)   '
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
               move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Ultima tratt. sindac.
           move  OC-LPUTRASIND       to  MBN021  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
           if  OC-LPUTRASIND  =  OC-FADTRATSIND
           then
               continue
           else
               move  'OC-LPUTRASIND  not=  OC-FADTRATSIND             '
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
               move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
           end-if.
      * 11.07.2017 RIPRISTINATO PER GESTIONE ACCONTO
      *----------------------------------------- Acconto
           move  OC-RECIMUREE-3      to  MBN023  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
           if  OC-FCODPAGA1    =  'ACC'
               if  OC-RECIMUREE-3  =  OC-FIMPPAGA1
               then
                   continue
               else
                   move  'OC-FIMPPAGA1   not=  OC-RECIMUREE-3         '
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
                   move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
               end-if
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Ultimo  recupero ind.
           add   OC-RECIMUREE-1      to  MBN024  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
           if  OC-FADRECSUIND  =  OC-RECIMUREE-1
           then
               continue
           else
               move  'OC-FADRECSUIND not=  OC-RECIMUREE-1             '
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
               move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Sommo recuperi      *
           add   OC-RECIMUREE-1      to  MBN013  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Ultimo  recupero ANF
           add   OC-RECIMUREE-2      to  MBN024  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
           if  OC-FADRECSUANF  =  OC-RECIMUREE-2
           then
               continue
           else
               move  'OC-FADRECSUANF not=  OC-RECIMUREE-2             '
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
               move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Sommo recuperi      *
           add   OC-RECIMUREE-2      to  MBN016  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Interessi indennità
      *    move  zeros               to  MBN025  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *    add   OC-***INLEPRE       to  MBN025  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Interessi ANF
      *    add   OC-***INLEANE       to  MBN025  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Assegno
      *---------------------------------conta   Pagamenti > 3000 euro
      *    IF    OC-FADNETTOPAG   > 3000
      *          ADD   1   TO  CTR-ATT-PAGME
      *    END-IF.
           move  OC-FADNETTOPAG      to  MBN026  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
       J24-EX.
           EXIT.
      *
       J26-SSTEURO.
      *----------------------------------------- Data riferim. calcol*
           move  OC-SSTULASS        to  W8-AAAAMMGG.
           move  W8-GG              to  D8-GG.
           move  W8-MM              to  D8-MM.
           move  W8-AAAA            to  D8-AAAA.
           move  D8-GGMMAAAA        to  MBN012  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Totale indennita'
           move  OC-SSTIMINT         to  MBN014  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *     add  OC-SSTIMRIN         to  MBN014  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Totale gg. indenn.
           move  OC-SSTGGCALC        to  MBN015  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Totale ANF    NO!
      *    move  OC-???IMANFT        to  MBN017  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *     add  OC-???MAGANFT       to  MBN017  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Totale gg. ANF
      *    move  OC-???ANFTOGG       to  MBN018  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Totale tratt. IRPEF AC
      *    move  OC-???TOIRNCE       to  MBN020  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Totale tratt. IRPEF AP
      *    move  OC-???TOIRNPE       to  MBN030  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Totale tratt. sindac.
      *    move  OC-???TOTRSIE       to  MBN022  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Ultimo importo ind.
           move  OC-SSTIMINU         to  MBN013  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
            add  OC-SSTIMRINU        to  MBN013  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
           if  (MBN013  of  VO-DSPFM13B  >  zeros)   and
               (OC-FCODPAGA1  =  'SNI')
           then
               if  (OC-SSTIMINU + OC-SSTIMRINU)  =
                            (OC-FACIMPONIBILE  +
                             OC-FAPIMPONIBILE  +
                             OC-FACTREDICESIMA +
                             OC-FIMPPAGA1)
               then
                   continue
               else
                   move
                     'OC-SSTIMINU not= OC-(FAC+FAPIMPONIBILE+FACTREDI)'
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
                   move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
               end-if
               if  OC-SSTIMRINU  =   OC-FACTREDICESIMA
               or                =   0
               then
                   continue
               else
                   move
                     'OC-SSTIMRINU not= OC-FACTREDICESIMA             '
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
                   move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
               end-if
           end-if.
           if  (MBN013  of  VO-DSPFM13B  >  zeros)  and
               (OC-FCODPAGA1  not =  'SNI')
           then
               if  (OC-SSTIMINU + OC-SSTIMRINU)  =
                            (OC-FACIMPONIBILE  +
                             OC-FAPIMPONIBILE  +
                             OC-FACTREDICESIMA)
               then
                   continue
               else
                   move
                     'OC-SSTIMINU not= OC-(FAC+FAPIMPONIBILE+FACTREDI)'
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
                   move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
               end-if
               if  OC-SSTIMRINU  =   OC-FACTREDICESIMA
               or                =   0
               then
                   continue
               else
                   move
                     'OC-SSTIMRINU not= OC-FACTREDICESIMA             '
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
                   move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
               end-if
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Indebito?           *
           if  MBN013  of  VO-DSPFM13B  =  zeros
           then
               move  OC-SSTINDEB     to  MBN013  of  VO-DSPFM13B
               multiply  -1          by  MBN013  of  VO-DSPFM13B
           end-if.
      *
      *    if  OC-SSTINDEB  >  zeros
      *    then
      *        if  OC-SSTINDEB   =
      *                       (OC-FACIMPONIBILE  +  OC-FAPIMPONIBILE)
      *        then
      *            continue
      *        else
      *            move
      *              'OC-SSTINDEB not= OC-(FAC+FAPIMPONIBILE)         '
      *                                              to  W-CHK-CAMPI
      *            move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
      *        end-if
      *    end-if.
      *--------------------------- no! --------- Ultimo importo ANF
      *    move  OC-???IMANFU        to  MBN016  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *     add  OC-???MAGANF        to  MBN016  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *    if  (OC-???IMANFU  +  OC-???MAGANF)  =  OC-FADANFPAGATI
      *    then
      *        continue
      *    else
      *        move  'OC-FADANFPAGATI not=  OC-(???IMANFU+???MAGANF)  '
      *                                              to  W-CHK-CAMPI
      *        move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
      *    end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Ultima tratt. IRPEF AC
           move  OC-FACIMPNETTA      to  MBN019  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
           if  OC-SSTIRPEFU  =  OC-FACIMPNETTA  +  OC-FAPIMPNETTA
           then
               continue
           else
               move  'OC-SSTIRPEFU not= OC-(FAC+FAPIMPNETTA)          '
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
               move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Ultima tratt. IRPEF AP
           move  OC-FAPIMPNETTA      to  MBN029  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Conguaglio Irpef AP
           if  OC-SSTCONGFIS  <  zeroes
           then
               string  'Rimborso   Irpef '   delimited  by  size
                       W4-ANNO-1             delimited  by  size
                                  into  MBA031  of  VO-DSPFM13B
               move  OC-SSTCONGFIS  to  MBN032  of  VO-DSPFM13B
           end-if.
           if  OC-SSTCONGFIS  >  zeroes
           then
               string  'Conguaglio Irpef '   delimited  by  size
                       W4-ANNO-1             delimited  by  size
                                  into  MBA031  of  VO-DSPFM13B
               move  OC-SSTCONGFIS  to  MBN032  of  VO-DSPFM13B
           end-if.
           if  OC-SSTCONGFIS  =  (OC-FCONGAC  +  OC-FCONGAP)
           then
               continue
           else
               move  'OC-SSTCONGFIS not= OC-FCONGAC + OC-FCONGAP      '
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
               move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Conguaglio Irpef 730
           if  OC-SSTCONG730  not =  zeroes
           then
               move  'Conguaglio da 730    '
                                    to  MBA031  of  VO-DSPFM13B
               move  OC-SSTCONG730  to  MBN032  of  VO-DSPFM13B
      *        if  OC-FCODPAGA1   =   '730'   and
      *            OC-SSTCONG730  =   OC-FIMPPAGA1
               if  OC-CODICE2     =   '730'   and
                   OC-SSTCONG730  =   OC-IMPORTO2
               then
                   continue
               else
      *        move  'OC-SSTCONG730 not= OC-FIMPPAGA1                 '
               move  'OC-SSTCONG730 not= OC-IMPORTO2                  '
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
                   move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
               end-if
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Addizionale Regionale
           move  OC-SSTADDIZR       to  MBN033  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
            add  OC-SSTADDIZRR      to  MBN033  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
           if  (OC-SSTADDIZR   +   OC-SSTADDIZRR)  =
                                 (OC-FIMPREGAC  +  OC-FIMPREGAP)
           then
               continue
           else
               move  'OC-SSTADDIZR  not= OC-(FIMPREGAC + FIMPREGAP)   '
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
               move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Addizionale Comunale
           move  OC-SSTADDIZC       to  MBN034  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
            add  OC-SSTADDIZRC      to  MBN034  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
           if  (OC-SSTADDIZC   +   OC-SSTADDIZRC)  =
                                 (OC-FIMPCOMAC  +  OC-FIMPCOMAP)
           then
               continue
           else
               move  'OC-SSTADDIZC  not= OC-(FIMPCOMAC + FIMPCOMAP)   '
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
               move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Ultima tratt. sindac.
           move  OC-SSTTRASIND       to  MBN021  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
           if  OC-SSTTRASIND  =  OC-FADTRATSIND
           then
               continue
           else
