                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
               move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
           end-if.
      * 11.07.2017 RIPRISTINATO PER GESTIONE ACCONTO
      *----------------------------------------- Acconto
           move  OC-RECIMUREE-3      to  MBN023  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
           if  OC-FCODPAGA1    =  'ACC'
               if  OC-RECIMUREE-3  =  OC-FIMPPAGA1
               then
                   continue
               else
                   move  'OC-FIMPPAGA1   not=  OC-RECIMUREE-3         '
                                                     to  W-CHK-CAMPI
                   move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
               end-if
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Ultimo  recupero ind.
           add   OC-RECIMUREE-1      to  MBN024  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
           if H-SSTIMRIN > 0
           and H-SSTCODIND NOT = 'FTCG'
           and H-SSTCODIND NOT = 'FTCD'
           and H-SSTCODIND NOT = 'FTCC'
           and H-SSTCODIND NOT = 'TRAC'
              add   OC-SSTRECRIN        to  MBN024  of  VO-DSPFM13B
              if  OC-FADRECSUIND  =  OC-RECIMUREE-1  +  OC-SSTRECRIN
              then
                continue
              else
                move  'OC-FADRECSUIND not=OC-RECIMUREE-1 + OC-SSTRECRIN'
                                                         to  W-CHK-CAMPI
                move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
              end-if
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Sommo recuperi      *
           add   OC-RECIMUREE-1      to  MBN013  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
           if H-SSTIMRIN > 0
           and H-SSTCODIND NOT = 'FTCG'
           and H-SSTCODIND NOT = 'FTCD'
           and H-SSTCODIND NOT = 'FTCC'
           and H-SSTCODIND NOT = 'TRAC'
               add   OC-SSTRECRIN        to  MBN013  of  VO-DSPFM13B
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Ultimo  recupero ANF
      *    add   OC-RECIMUREE-2      to  MBN024  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *    if  OC-FADRECSUANF  =  OC-RECIMUREE-2
      *    then
      *        continue
      *    else
      *        move  'OC-FADRECSUANF not=  OC-RECIMUREE-2             '
      *                                              to  W-CHK-CAMPI
      *        move  'S'  to  W-ERRORE
      *    end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Sommo recuperi      *
      *    add   OC-RECIMUREE-2      to  MBN016  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Interessi indennità
      *    move  zeros               to  MBN025  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *    add   OC-***INLEPRE       to  MBN025  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Interessi ANF
      *    add   OC-***INLEANE       to  MBN025  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *---------------------------------conta   Pagamenti > 3000 euro
      *    IF    OC-FADNETTOPAG      > 3000
      *          ADD   1   TO  CTR-ATT-PAGME
      *    END-IF.
      *----------------------------------------- Assegno
           move  OC-FADNETTOPAG      to  MBN026  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
       J26-EX.
           EXIT.
      *
       J30-MUOVILIRE.
      *----------------------------------------- Tipo prestazione    *
           if  W-CODICEDUE  =  42
           then
               perform  J32-ASULIRE     thru  J32-EX
           end-if.
           if  W-CODICEDUE  =  44
           then
               perform  J34-LPULIRE     thru  J34-EX
           end-if.
           if  W-CODICEDUE  =  45
           then
               perform  J36-SSTLIRE     thru  J36-EX
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Squadratura
           if  W-NIK  =  'S'
           then
               if  W-DIFFERENZA     =  zeros
               then
                   move  spaces     to  MBA041  of  VO-DSPFM13B
               else
                   move  'Attenzione: squadratura!         '
                                to  MBA041  of  VO-DSPFM13B
                   go  to  J30-EX
               end-if
               if  W-CHK-CAMPI       =  spaces
               then
                   move  spaces     to  MBA041  of  VO-DSPFM13B
               else
                   move  'Attenzione: dati calcolo dubbi!  '
                                to  MBA041  of  VO-DSPFM13B
               end-if
           end-if.
       J30-EX.
           EXIT.
      *
       J32-ASULIRE.
           move  OC-ASUULASS        to  W8-AAAAMMGG.
           move  W8-GG              to  D8-GG.
           move  W8-MM              to  D8-MM.
           move  W8-AAAA            to  D8-AAAA.
           move  D8-GGMMAAAA        to  MBN012  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Totale indennita'
           compute  W-CALCOLI   rounded  =
                                    OC-ASUIMINT      *  W-EURO.
           move  W-CALCOLI          to  MBN014  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Totale gg. indenn.
           move  OC-ASUGGCALC        to  MBN015  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Totale ANF
           compute  W-CALCOLI   rounded  =
                                    OC-ASUIMANFT     *  W-EURO.
           move  W-CALCOLI          to  MBN017  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
           compute  W-CALCOLI   rounded  =
                                    OC-ASUMAGANFT    *  W-EURO.
            add  W-CALCOLI          to  MBN017  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Totale gg. ANF
      *    move  OC-???ANFTOGG       to  MBN018  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Totale tratt. IRPEF AC
      *    compute  W-CALCOLI   rounded  =
      *                             OC-???TOIRNCE    *  W-EURO.
      *    move  W-CALCOLI          to  MBN020  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Totale tratt. IRPEF AP
      *    compute  W-CALCOLI   rounded  =
      *                             OC-PMETOIRNPE    *  W-EURO.
      *    move  W-CALCOLI          to  MBN030  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Totale tratt. sindac.
      *    compute  W-CALCOLI   rounded  =
      *                             OC-???TOTRSIE    *  W-EURO.
      *    move  W-CALCOLI          to  MBN022  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Ultimo importo ind.
           compute  W-CALCOLI   rounded  =
                                    OC-ASUIMINU      *  W-EURO.
           move  W-CALCOLI          to  MBN013  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Ultimo importo ANF
           compute  W-CALCOLI   rounded  =
                                    OC-ASUIMANFU     *  W-EURO.
           move  W-CALCOLI          to  MBN016  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
           compute  W-CALCOLI   rounded  =
                                    OC-ASUMAGANF     *  W-EURO.
            add  W-CALCOLI          to  MBN016  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Ultima tratt. IRPEF AC
           compute  W-CALCOLI   rounded  =
                                    OC-FACIMPNETTA   *  W-EURO.
           move  W-CALCOLI          to  MBN019  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Ultima tratt. IRPEF AP
           compute  W-CALCOLI   rounded  =
                                    OC-FAPIMPNETTA   *  W-EURO.
           move  W-CALCOLI          to  MBN029  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Conguaglio Irpef AC
      *    if  OC- CONGAC ???  ><  zeroes
      *    then
      *        move  'Conguaglio Irpef A.C.'
      *    o    move  'Rimborso D.L.268/2000'
      *                             to  MBA031  of  VO-DSPFM13B
      *    end-if.
      *    compute  W-CALCOLI   rounded  =
      *                             OC- CONGAC ???  *  W-EURO.
      *    move  W-CALCOLI          to  MBN032  of  VO-DSPFM13B.
      *----------------------------------------- Conguaglio Irpef AP
           if  OC-ASUCONGFIS  <  zeroes
           then
               string  'Rimborso   Irpef '   delimited  by  size
                       W4-ANNO-1             delimited  by  size
                                  into  MBA031  of  VO-DSPFM13B
               compute  W-CALCOLI   rounded  =
                                    OC-ASUCONGFIS    *  W-EURO
               move  W-CALCOLI      to  MBN032  of  VO-DSPFM13B
           end-if.
           if  OC-ASUCONGFIS  >  zeroes
           then
               string  'Conguaglio Irpef '   delimited  by  size
                       W4-ANNO-1             delimited  by  size
                                  into  MBA031  of  VO-DSPFM13B
               compute  W-CALCOLI   rounded  =
                                    OC-ASUCONGFIS    *  W-EURO
               move  W-CALCOLI      to  MBN032  of  VO-DSPFM13B
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Conguaglio 730      *
           if  OC-ASUCONG730  not  =  zeroes
           then
               move  'Conguaglio da 730    '
                                    to  MBA031  of  VO-DSPFM13B
               compute  W-CALCOLI   rounded  =
                                    OC-ASUCONG730    *  W-EURO
               move  W-CALCOLI      to  MBN032  of  VO-DSPFM13B
           end-if.
      *----------------------------------------- Addizionale Regionale
           compute  W-CALCOLI   rounded  =

       B20-DB2-FETCH.
      *
           IF WK-CURS = '1'
              IF KLIVAUTO = '5'
                EXEC SQL
                 FETCH CURSSCO1
                  INTO
                   :H-DCOCODFIS,
                   :H-DCOCENOPE,
                   :H-DCOCOTIDO,
                   :H-DCOCHIDOM,
                   :H-DCOPENS,
                   :H-DCOANFRIC,
                   :H-DCOANVEPR,
                   :H-DCONDVEPR,
                   :H-DCOULESPP,
                   :H-DCODTULPP,
                   :H-DCOULESSP,
                   :H-DCODTULSP,
                   :H-DCODTPRDO,
                   :H-DCODTDECPP,
                   :H-DCODTDECSP,
                   :H-DCOCODPAT,
                   :H-DCOZONPAT,
                   :H-DCOMODARR,
                   :H-DCOCOOBAN,
                   :H-DCOCOREIM,
                   :H-DCOTRDOCE,
                   :H-DCODTCODO,
                   :H-DCODTVIR,
                   :H-DCOINT,
                   :H-DCORECNUO,
                   :H-DCODTADEC,
                   :H-DCOPESTDI,
                   :H-DCOTRDODO,
                   :H-DCOCOERMI,
                   :H-DCODORICO,
                   :H-DCOFLASU,
                   :H-DCONUPRO,
                   :H-DCOIBAN
                END-EXEC
              ELSE
                EXEC SQL
                 FETCH CURSDCO1
                  INTO
                   :H-DCOCODFIS,
                   :H-DCOCENOPE,
                   :H-DCOCOTIDO,
                   :H-DCOCHIDOM,
                   :H-DCOPENS,
                   :H-DCOANFRIC,
                   :H-DCOANVEPR,
                   :H-DCONDVEPR,
                   :H-DCOULESPP,
                   :H-DCODTULPP,
                   :H-DCOULESSP,
                   :H-DCODTULSP,
                   :H-DCODTPRDO,
                   :H-DCODTDECPP,
                   :H-DCODTDECSP,
                   :H-DCOCODPAT,
                   :H-DCOZONPAT,
                   :H-DCOMODARR,
                   :H-DCOCOOBAN,
                   :H-DCOCOREIM,
                   :H-DCOTRDOCE,
                   :H-DCODTCODO,
                   :H-DCODTVIR,
                   :H-DCOINT,
                   :H-DCORECNUO,
                   :H-DCODTADEC,
                   :H-DCOPESTDI,
                   :H-DCOTRDODO,
                   :H-DCOCOERMI,
                   :H-DCODORICO,
                   :H-DCOFLASU,
                   :H-DCONUPRO,
                   :H-DCOIBAN
              END-EXEC
              END-IF
           END-IF.

                 EXEC SQL

      ******************************************************************
      *      UPDATE
      ******************************************************************
      *
       E39-DB2-COM-UPD.
      *
           MOVE  L-CODICE-SEDE    TO    H-DCOCOSEGR.
      *
           EXEC SQL
           UPDATE    TDSDATCO
            SET
                    H_DCOULESSP     = :H-DCOULESSP,
                    H_DCODTULSP     = :H-DCODTULSP,
                    H_DCOTRDOCE     = :H-DCOTRDOCE,
                    H_DCODTADEC     = :H-DCODTADEC,
                    H_DCOTRDODO     = :H-DCOTRDODO

              WHERE
                     H_DCOCHIDOM      =  :H-DCOCHIDOM
                AND  H_DCOCOSEGR      =  :H-DCOCOSEGR
           END-EXEC.
      *
           move  SQLCODE               to  FST-LFDATCO2.

           IF  SQLCODE NOT = 0
                 move  'N'                to  FLG-COMMIT
                 move  'REWRITE   '       to  S2A005
                 move  'LFDATCO2  '       to  S2A006
                 move  SQLCODE            to  S2A007
                 perform  S10-STAMPA     thru  S10-EX
           END-IF.
      *
       E39-DB2-COM-UPD-EX.
           EXIT.
      *
       E44-DB2-REC-UPD.
      *
           MOVE  L-CODICE-SEDE    TO    H-RECCOSEDE.
      *
           EXEC SQL
           UPDATE  TDSRECUP
            SET
                H_RECTORERE     = :H-RECTORERE,
                H_RECIMUREE     = :H-RECIMUREE,
                H_RECDTESRE     = :H-RECDTESRE
             WHERE
                     H_RECCHIDOM      =  :H-RECCHIDOM
                AND  H_RECPROREC      =  :H-RECPROREC
                AND  H_RECCOSEDE      =  :H-RECCOSEDE
           END-EXEC.
      *
           move  SQLCODE               to  FST-ADSRECUP.

           IF  SQLCODE NOT = 0
                 move  'N'                to  FLG-COMMIT
                 move  'REWRITE   '       to  S2A005
                 move  'ADSRECUP  '       to  S2A006
                 move  SQLCODE            to  S2A007
                 perform  S10-STAMPA     thru  S10-EX
           END-IF.
      *
       E44-DB2-REC-UPD-EX.
           EXIT.

      *
       E47-DB2-SIT-UPD.
      *
           MOVE  L-CODICE-SEDE    TO    H-STDCOSEDE.
      *
           EXEC SQL
           UPDATE   TDSSITDO
            SET
                H_STDDTMOPRD     = :H-STDDTMOPRD,
                H_STDESITPRD     = :H-STDESITPRD
             WHERE
                     H_STDCHIDOM      =  :H-STDCHIDOM
                AND  H_STDCOSEDE      =  :H-STDCOSEDE
           END-EXEC.
      *
           move  SQLCODE               to  FST-ADSSITDO.

           IF  SQLCODE NOT = 0
                 move  'N'                to  FLG-COMMIT
                 move  'REWRITE   '       to  S2A005
                 move  'ADSSITDO  '       to  S2A006
                 move  SQLCODE            to  S2A007
                 perform  S10-STAMPA     thru  S10-EX
           END-IF.
      *
       E47-DB2-SIT-UPD-EX.
           EXIT.
      *
       E64-DB2-UPDATE.
      *
           MOVE  L-CODICE-SEDE    TO    H-PCOSEDE.
           MOVE 'E64-DB2-UPDATE'  TO WABNDB-LABEL.
      *
           EXEC SQL
           UPDATE TDSRPG00
           SET
               H_PCALCOLATI        =  :H-PCALCOLATI,
               H_PZEROPAGAM        =  :H-PZEROPAGAM
            WHERE
                     H_PCOSEDE        =  :H-PCOSEDE
                AND  H_PDATAELABO     =  :H-PDATAELABO
                AND  H_PPROCEDURA     =  :H-PPROCEDURA
                AND  H_PPROGRESSI     =  :H-PPROGRESSI
                AND  H_PSTRUTTURA     =  :H-PSTRUTTURA
           END-EXEC.
      *
           move  SQLCODE               to  FST-ADSRPG00.
      *
           IF SQLCODE NOT = ZERO AND NOT = 100
               DISPLAY 'DCLTDSRPG00=' DCLTDSRPG00
               MOVE 'TDSRPG00'    TO  WABNDB-TABL
               MOVE 'update '     TO  WABNDB-FUNC
               PERFORM ERRORE-SQL
           END-IF.
      *
       E64-DB2-UPDATE-EX.
           EXIT.

              FROM TDSDATCO

                     H_DCOANVEPR      =  :H-DCOANVEPR
                AND  H_DCONDVEPR      =  :H-DCONDVEPR
                AND  H_DCOCOSEGR      =  :H-DCOCOSEGR
           END-EXEC.
           move  SQLCODE               to  FST-LFDATCO2.
      *
           IF SQLCODE NOT = ZERO AND NOT = 100
               DISPLAY 'DCLTDSDATCO=' DCLTDSDATCO
               MOVE 'TDSDATCO'    TO  WABNDB-TABL
               MOVE 'SELECT '     TO  WABNDB-FUNC
               PERFORM ERRORE-SQL

      *
           MOVE 'E62-DB2-SELECT'  TO WABNDB-LABEL.

      *

           SELECT
                H_PBACKUP,

                H_PFINEPAGAM,

           INTO
                :H-PBACKUP   ,
                :H-PCALCOLOAL,
                :H-PCALCOLATI,
                :H-PRECPAGATI,
                :H-PFINEPAGAM,
                :H-PZEROPAGAM,
                :H-PIMPCONTAB,
                :H-PIMPTELEMA,
                :H-PCODTELEMA,

              WHERE
                     H_PCOSEDE        =  :H-PCOSEDE
                AND  H_PDATAELABO     =  :H-PDATAELABO
                AND  H_PPROCEDURA     =  :H-PPROCEDURA
                AND  H_PPROGRESSI     =  :H-PPROGRESSI
                AND  H_PSTRUTTURA     =  :H-PSTRUTTURA
           END-EXEC.
           move  SQLCODE               to  FST-ADSRPG00.

               MOVE 'SELECT '     TO  WABNDB-FUNC

      ******************************************************************
      *       DELETE
      ******************************************************************
      *
       E45-DB2-DELETE.
      *
           MOVE  L-CODICE-SEDE    TO    H-PEECOSEDE.
      *
            EXEC SQL
            DELETE  FROM TDSPEERE
               WHERE
                H_PEECHIDOM =  :H-PEECHIDOM
            AND H_PEECOSEDE =  :H-PEECOSEDE
           END-EXEC .
           move  SQLCODE               to  FST-LFPEERE1.

           IF  SQLCODE  =  ZERO or = 100
               NEXT SENTENCE
           ELSE
               move  'N'              to  FLG-COMMIT
               move  'DELETE    '     to  S2A005
               move  'LFPEERE1  '     to  S2A006
               move  SQLCODE          to  S2A007
               perform  S10-STAMPA   thru  S10-EX
               move  111  to  NDC3
           END-IF.
      *
       E45-DB2-DELETE-EX.
           exit.
      *
      ******************************************************************
      *       INSERT
      ******************************************************************
      *
      * INSERIMENTO RIGA DI STAMPA
      *
       S30-INSERT-REPORT.
      *
           MOVE  'S30-INSERT-REPORT     '  TO  WABNDB-LABEL.
      *
           EXEC SQL
                   INSERT  INTO TDSREPOR
                   VALUES  (:DCLTDSREPOR)
           END-EXEC.
      *
           IF    SQLCODE NOT = ZERO
                   DISPLAY 'DCLTDSREPOR=' DCLTDSREPOR
                   MOVE 'TDSREPOR' TO WABNDB-TABL
                   MOVE 'INSERT  ' TO WABNDB-FUNC
                   PERFORM ERRORE-SQL
110523     ELSE
110523       IF LMATRICOLA = 'E0000419' or '50000419'
110523         DISPLAY 'ELENA-PDSIO13-TDSREPOR: ' DCLTDSREPOR
110523         DISPLAY 'ELENA-PDSIO13-OCMESSAGGIO: ' OC-MESSAGGIO
110523       END-IF
           END-IF.
      *
       S30-EX-INSERT-REPORT.
      *
           EXIT.
      *
       E46-DB2-EFFE-INS.
      *
           MOVE  L-CODICE-SEDE    TO    H-PEECOSEDE.
      *
           EXEC SQL
                   INSERT  INTO TDSPEERE
                   VALUES  ( :DCLTDSPEERE)
           END-EXEC.
      *
           move  SQLCODE               to  FST-LFPEERE1.

           IF    SQLCODE not = ZERO
                   move  'N'                to  FLG-COMMIT
                   move  'WRITE     '       to  S2A005
                   move  'LFPEERE1  '       to  S2A006
                   move  SQLCODE            to  S2A007
                   perform  S10-STAMPA     thru  S10-EX
           END-IF.
      *
       E46-DB2-EFFE-INS-EX.
              EXIT.
      *
       E30-DB2-INSERT.
      *
           MOVE  'E30-DB2-INSERT '  TO  WABNDB-LABEL.
           MOVE  L-CODICE-SEDE    TO    H-O0COSEDE.
      *
           EXEC SQL

      *
           IF    SQLCODE NOT = ZERO
                   DISPLAY 'DCLTDSAPIO0=' DCLTDSAPIO0

                   PERFORM ERRORE-SQL
           END-IF.
           move  SQLCODE               to  FST-ADSAPIO0.
      *
       E30-DB2-INSERT-EX.
              EXIT.
      *
       E40-DB2-FI40-INS.
      *
           MOVE  'E40-DB2-FI40-INS' TO  WABNDB-LABEL.
      *
           if IC-DCOCOTIDO = 'E'
           then
              MOVE  '0000'           TO    CODSAP OF DCLTDSASU
           else
              move  L-CODICE-SEDE    TO    CODSAP OF DCLTDSASU
           end-if.
      *

                   VALUES  ( :DCLTDSASU )
           END-EXEC.
      *

      *    IF    SQLCODE not = ZERO
      *            move  'N'                to  FLG-COMMIT

      *            move  SQLCODE            to  S2A007
      *            PERFORM S10-STAMPA      thru  S10-EX
      *    END-IF.
      *
       E40-DB2-FI40-INS-EX.
              EXIT.
      *
       E47A-DB2-FI47-INS.
      *
           MOVE  L-CODICE-SEDE    TO    CODSAP OF DCLTDSLIST.
      *
           EXEC SQL
                   INSERT  INTO        TDSLIST
                   VALUES  ( :DCLTDSLIST )
           END-EXEC.
      *
           move  SQLCODE               to  FST-ADSASU7.

           IF    SQLCODE not = ZERO
                   move  'N'                to  FLG-COMMIT
                   move  'WRITE     '       to  S2A005
                   move  'TDSLIST   '       to  S2A006
                   move  SQLCODE            to  S2A007
                                                FST-ADSLIST
                   DISPLAY 'TDSLIST SQLCODE= '  FST-ADSLIST
                   PERFORM S10-STAMPA      thru  S10-EX
           END-IF.

              EXIT.

              WHERE
                    ANNODEL           =  :DCLTDSLIST.ANNODEL
                AND CFLAV             =  :DCLTDSLIST.CFLAV
                AND CODFIS            =  :DCLTDSLIST.CODFIS
                AND NUMDEL            =  :DCLTDSLIST.NUMDEL
           END-EXEC.

           IF  SQLCODE NOT = 0

                   move  'TDSLIST   '       to  S2A006
                   move  SQLCODE            to  S2A007
                   PERFORM S10-STAMPA      thru  S10-EX
           END-IF.
      *
       E47A-DB2-FI47-UPD-EX.
           EXIT.

       IMPOSTA-RPT.
      *
           MOVE  'IMPOSTA-RPT'  TO  WABNDB-LABEL.
      *
           MOVE FUNCTION CURRENT-DATE(1:14) TO WK-TIMESTAMP-DATA-ORA.
           MOVE WK-GG      TO  WW-DB2-GG.
           MOVE WK-MM      TO  WW-DB2-MM.
           MOVE WK-AA      TO  WW-DB2-AA.
           MOVE WK-H       TO  WW-DB2-HH
241023                         W-T-HH.
           MOVE WK-M       TO  WW-DB2-T-MM
241023                         W-T-MM.
           MOVE WK-S       TO  WW-DB2-SS.
           MOVE WK-DB2-DATA   TO TDSREPORT-DTA-PRE.
           MOVE WK-DB2-TIME   TO TDSREPORT-ORA-PRE.
           MOVE 0             TO TDSREPORT-NUM-RIGA.
           MOVE SPACES        TO TDSREPORT-RIGA-REPORT.
           MOVE L-CODICE-SEDE TO TDSREPORT-SEDE.
           MOVE L-CODICE-STOP TO TDSREPORT-CEOP.
           MOVE L-PROCEDURA   TO TDSREPORT-PROCEDURA.
           MOVE KMATRICOLA    TO TDSREPORT-MATRICOLA.
      *
           MOVE TDSREPORT-SEDE      TO WK-RPT-SEDE.
           MOVE TDSREPORT-CEOP      TO WK-RPT-CEOP.
           MOVE TDSREPORT-MATRICOLA TO WK-RPT-MATRICOLA.
           MOVE TDSREPORT-DTA-PRE   TO WK-RPT-DTA-PRE.
           MOVE TDSREPORT-ORA-PRE   TO WK-RPT-ORA-PRE.
      *
       EX-IMPOSTA-RPT.
           EXIT.

           MOVE WK-DATA-AAAA                  TO W8-AAAA.
           MOVE WK-DATA-MM                    TO W8-MM  .
           MOVE WK-DATA-GG                    TO W8-GG  .
      *
